#supply from sov
country_event = {
	id = prc.1
	title = prc.1.t
	desc = prc.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_tanks
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = prc_1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = "PRC_sov_supply"
			random_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Su-lien Yüan-ping\" division_template = \"Su-lien Chih-yüan-chün\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 1 force_equipment_variants = { infantry_equipment_1 = { owner = SOV } }	"
					OWNER = PRC
					prioritize_location = 12356
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no  
					count = 3
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Su-lien Yüan-ping\" division_template = \"T'an-k'o Pu-tui\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 1 force_equipment_variants = { infantry_equipment_1 = { owner = SOV } } "
					OWNER = PRC
					prioritize_location = 12356
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no  
					count = 1
				}
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 3000 producer = SOV }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = 2200 producer = SOV }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = light_tank_chassis_1 amount = 310 producer = SOV }
	}
}

#more skilled people
country_event = {
	id = prc.4
	title = prc.4.t
	desc = prc.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_physics_lab_02
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.4.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = prc_msp_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
			}
			remove_ideas = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
			add_research_slot = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = prc.4 days = 30 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = prc.4 days = 30 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = prc.4 days = 30 }

				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_6

		}
		if = {

				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_3
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_4
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = prc.4 days = 30 }
			}

#Stalin pass away
country_event = {
	id = prc.5
	title = prc.5.t
	desc = prc.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				PRC = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				date > 1953.3.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1945.10.15
				has_war = no
				PRC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1948.5.1
				has_war = yes
				PRC = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		tag = SOV
		NOT = { has_country_flag = counter_purge }
		has_government = communism
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			news_event = { id = kns.4 hours = 5 }
			country_event = { id = prc.31 days = 600 }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Vacant Position"
				desc = "POLITICS_PS_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/SOV/portrait_SOV_supreme_soviet.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = marxism
				traits = {
					sov_power_truggle
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = stalin_dead
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.5.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = sov_power_struggle_begins
	}
}

#Hai Rui Ba gUan
country_event = {
	id = prc.6
	title = prc.6.t
	desc = prc.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_journalists_speech
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_war = no
		has_country_flag = KMT_leap_stop
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = stalin_dead
			SOV = { 
				NOT = { 
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SOV_iosif_stalin
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = { is_puppet = yes }
			SOV = { NOT = { has_government = communism }}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 300 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = PRC_hairuibaguan
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.6.a
	}
}

		}
	}

#Lin biao's fate
country_event = {
	id = prc.9
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_global_flag = mao_assassin_event_fired
		has_global_flag = PRC_lin_choice_fired
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = mao_dead
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = lin_biao_fate_fired
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = linbiao_must_die
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					save_event_target_as = PRC_linbiao_flee_target
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_country = {
									NOT = { 
										tag = ROOT
										is_puppet_of = ROOT
									}
									exists = yes
								}
							}
						}
						set_global_flag = one_China_flag
						else = {
							random_other_country = {
								limit = {
									exists = yes
									NOT = {
										is_puppet_of = ROOT
									}
								}
								save_event_target_as = PRC_linbiao_flee_target
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					85 = {
						country_event = {
							id = prc.8 
						}
					}
					15 = {
						country_event = {
							id = prc.10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_historical_focus_on = no
				}
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						country_event = {
							id = prc.8 
						}
					}
					40 = {
						country_event = {
							id = prc.10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = prc.8 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

#death of mao ze dong
country_event = {
	id = prc.12
	title = prc.12.t
	desc = prc.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_global_flag = lin_biao_fate_fired
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = mao_assassinated
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 80 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			remove_unit_leader = 1064
			PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_dead
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_fled_to_soviet
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Hua Kuo-feng"
					desc = "POLITICS_HUA_GUO_FENG_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/Asia/Portrait_Asia_Generic_communism.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = marxism
					traits = {
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = huaguofeng
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_dead
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_fled_to_soviet
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					PRC_lin_biao = { 
						set_nationality = PRC 
					}
				}
				PRC_lin_biao = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Lin_Biao_back.dds" }
						army = { large = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Lin_Biao_back.dds" }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
					promote_character = { ideology = marxism }
				}
				set_country_flag = lin_biao
				add_political_power = 500
				add_manpower = -5750000
				remove_ideas = PRC_cultural_revolution
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = PRC_cultural_revolution_aftermath
					days = 600
				}
				set_global_flag = CR_ended
			}
			add_stability = -0.075
			set_global_flag = mao_dead
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.12.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.075
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_dead
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_fled_to_soviet
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Hua Kuo-feng"
					ideology = marxism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_dead
						has_global_flag = lin_biao_fled_to_soviet
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Lin Piao"
					ideology = marxism
				}
				add_political_power = 500
				add_manpower = -5750000
				remove_ideas = PRC_cultural_revolution
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = PRC_cultural_revolution_aftermath
					days = 600
				}
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 1064
		}
	}
}

#economic reform foreign investment
country_event = {
	id = prc.14
	title = prc.14.t
	desc = prc.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_second_vienna_award_pact
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		focus_progress = {
			progress > 0.1
			focus = PRC_economic_reform
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	immediate = {
		every_other_country = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PRC
				modifier = PRC_swcc_2
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.14.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 2
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 4
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = prc_more_trade_deals_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = PRC_socialism_with_chinese_characteristics
			add_ideas = PRC_socialism_with_chinese_characteristics_2
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = prc.14.t
	desc = prc.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_second_vienna_award_pact
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		focus_progress = {
			progress > 0.7
			focus = PRC_economic_reform
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_other_country = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PRC
				modifier = PRC_swcc_4
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.14.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 2
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 4
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = prc_more_trade_deals_and_construct_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = PRC_socialism_with_chinese_characteristics_4
			add_ideas = PRC_socialism_with_chinese_characteristics_5
		}
	}
}

					has_tech = tech_support
				}
			}
			set_technology = { tech_support = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = tech_field_hospital
				NOT = {
					has_tech = tech_field_hospital2
				}
			}
			set_technology = { tech_field_hospital2 = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = tech_field_hospital
				}
			}
			set_technology = { tech_field_hospital = 1 }
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = 500 producer = PRC }
	}
}

#event for integration of government
country_event = {
	id = prc.32
	title = prc.32.t
	desc = prc.32.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = prc.32.a
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.33 }
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				change_tag_from = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_character_flag = KMT_temp_sn_flag
			set_nationality = FROM
		}
		every_character = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = KMT_temp_sn_flag }
			set_nationality = FROM
			clr_character_flag = KMT_temp_sn_flag
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
			}
			add_core_of = FROM
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_claimed_by = FROM }
			}
			add_claim_by = FROM
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.32.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ROOT
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = prc.34 }}
		add_timed_idea = {
			days = 1000
			idea = PRC_defiant
		}
	}
}

		set_global_flag = mao_assassin_event_fired

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = mao_must_die
			}
			country_event = { id = prc.46 }
			else = {
				random_list = {
					95 = {
						country_event = { id = prc.47 }
					}
					5 = {
						country_event = { id = prc.46 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

#assassination of mao - success
country_event = {
	id = prc.46
	title = prc.46.t
	desc = prc.46.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			every_country = {
				PRC_lin_biao = { 
					set_nationality = PRC 
				}
			}
			PRC_lin_biao = { 
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Lin_Biao_back.dds" }
					army = { large = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Lin_Biao_back.dds" }
				}
				promote_leader = yes
				promote_character = { ideology = marxism }
			}
			set_country_flag = lin_biao
			set_country_flag = mao_assassinated
			set_global_flag = mao_dead
			add_stability = -0.1
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = 500
				add_manpower = -1750000
				remove_ideas = PRC_cultural_revolution
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = PRC_cultural_revolution_aftermath
					days = 600
				}
				set_global_flag = CR_ended
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.46.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Lin Piao"
				ideology = marxism
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = 500
				add_manpower = -5750000
				remove_ideas = PRC_cultural_revolution
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = PRC_cultural_revolution_aftermath
					days = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#zhang xueliang agree to join the grand northwest united
country_event = {
	id = prc.57
	title = prc.57.t
	desc = prc.57.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_army_training
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = zxl_as_gnwu_leader
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PRC_no_wargoal_to_chi_when_ok
			}
			set_global_flag = PRC_no_wargoal_to_chi_with_gnwu
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = PRC_west_expedition
				NSM = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NSM = {
						is_puppet = yes
					}
				}
				NSM = {
					overlord = {
						save_event_target_as = PRC_overlord_of_NSM
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = event_target:PRC_overlord_of_NSM
					type = take_state_focus
					generator = {283}
				}
				else = {
					create_wargoal = {
						target = NSM
						type = take_core_state
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.57.a
		
		annex_country = {
			target = ZXL
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ZXL = { ZXL_zhang_xueliang = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_li_bo_hai = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_he_zhuguo = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_yu_xuezhong = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_wang_tehan = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_xu_lanzhou = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_mazhanshan = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
			ZXL = { ZXL_liu_duo_quan = { set_nationality = ROOT }}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = prc.66
	title = prc.66.t
	desc = prc.66.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_purge_speech
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = PRC
		SOV = {
			has_country_flag = counter_purge
			has_government = communism
		}
		has_government = communism
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_zxl_purge
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.66.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = ZXL_zhang_xueliang
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ch'en Tu-hsiu"
				desc = "POLITICS_CHEN_DUXIU_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Portrait_Chen_Duxiu.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = leninism
				traits = {
					PRC_trotskyist
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = PRC_enable_cdx
				custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
				show_ideas_tooltip = PRC_chen_duxiu
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = cdx_returned
		remove_unit_leader = 1064
			hidden_effect = { PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		name = prc.66.b
		add_opinion_modifier = { 
			target = SOV
			modifier = trostkyism_vermin
		}
	}
}

				factor = 1
			}
		}
		name = prc.67.a
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.68 }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 621
						state = 966
						state = 746
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { 
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}							
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.69 }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = take_core_state
				generator = { 621 746 966 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = prc.77.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		clr_global_flag = PRC_defy_sov_order
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PRC
			modifier = PRC_defy_order
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PRC
			modifier = PRC_defy_order_2
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.78 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons
							NOT = {
								has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 1000 producer = SOV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							NOT = {
								has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 1000 producer = SOV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							NOT = {
								has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_2 amount = 1000 producer = SOV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = {
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_3 amount = 1000 producer = SOV }
				}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = prc.77.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.79 }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = prc.92.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.25
				}
				add = -25
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.5
				}
				add = -25
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.75
				}
				add = -25
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1
				}
				add = -25
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			end_puppet = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_together_with = FROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = democratic
					}
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							has_government = democratic
							has_war = no
							exists = yes
						}
						puppet = ROOT
						end_puppet = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_country = {
									NOT = { tag = ROOT }
									has_government = democratic
								}
							}
						}
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								has_war = no
								exists = yes
							}
							puppet = ROOT
							end_puppet = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
							has_war = no
							exists = yes
						}
						puppet = ROOT
						end_puppet = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_country = {
									NOT = { tag = ROOT }
									has_government = communism
								}
							}
						}
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								has_war = no
								exists = yes
							}
							puppet = ROOT
							end_puppet = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							has_government = fascism
							has_war = no
							exists = yes
						}
						puppet = ROOT
						end_puppet = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_country = {
									NOT = { tag = ROOT }
									has_government = fascism
								}
							}
						}
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								has_war = no
								exists = yes
							}
							puppet = ROOT
							end_puppet = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							has_government = neutrality
							has_war = no
							exists = yes
						}
						puppet = ROOT
						end_puppet = ROOT
					}
					if = {

								}
							}
						}

								exists = yes
							}
							puppet = ROOT
							end_puppet = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

					}

				add = 20
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			puppet = ROOT

		}
	}

	option = {
		name = prc.87.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.100 }

			}
		}

#blitzkrieg
country_event = {
	id = prc.131
	title = prc.131.t
	desc = prc.131.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_soviet_tanks
	
	trigger = {
		SOV = {
			has_war = yes
			surrender_progress > 0.25
		}
		has_war = no
		tag = SIK
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_war_together_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				is_puppet_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			}
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
				has_war_together_with = SOV
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
					surrender_progress > 0.8
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = prc.131.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.9
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PRC = { has_government = communism }
				}
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = prc.133 }
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = prc.134 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					SIK = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
				}
				remove_from_faction = SIK
			}
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			country_event = { id = prc.132 hours = 5 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_together_with = SOV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = { end_puppet = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
			}
			SOV = { remove_from_faction = ROOT }
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SOV
			type = annex_everything
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = prc.144 }
		}
		name = prc.131.b
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5 
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = prc.131.c
	}
}

#blitskrieg
country_event = {
	id = prc.132
	title = prc.132.t
	desc = prc.132.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = prc.132.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			puppet = FROM
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = PRC_sik_issue_opi
			}
			country_event = { id = prc.143 }
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.141 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				SIK = { NOT = { has_character = XIA_zhang_zhizhong }}
				any_country = {
					NOT = { tag = PRC }
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						tag = ROOT
					}
					has_character = XIA_zhang_zhizhong
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { tag = PRC }
					has_character = XIA_zhang_zhizhong 
				}
				XIA_zhang_zhizhong = { set_nationality = SIK }
			}
			SIK = {	
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					character = XIA_zhang_zhizhong
					ideology = despotism
				}
				XIA_zhang_zhizhong = { 
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1999.1.1"
							ideology = despotism
							traits = {  }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			SIK = { SIK_wu_zhongxin = { promote_character = { ideology = despotism }}}
		}
		SIK = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality name = SIK_provincial_government long_name = SIK_provincial_government }
			if = { limit = { has_character = SIK_sheng_shicai } retire_character = SIK_sheng_shicai }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = prc.132.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.142 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = prc.149
	title = prc.149.t
	desc = prc.149.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { tag = SIK }
			is_subject_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
		is_valid_power_struggle_participant = yes
		OR = {
			any_owned_state = {
				any_neighbor_state = {
					controller = {
						tag = PRC
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned_state = {
				any_neighbor_state = {
					PRC = {
						divisions_in_state = {
							state = PREV
							size > 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned_state = {
				PRC = {
					divisions_in_state = {
						state = PREV
						size > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = { NOT = { tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag }}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			has_war_with = PRC
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = prc149_fired
			has_idea = KMT_ccw_ceasefire
		}
		PRC = { 
			num_of_controlled_states > 10
			NOT = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
		}
		has_global_flag = {
			flag = PRC_restart_CHI_war
			days > 200
		}

		has_capitulated = no

		set_country_flag = prc149_fired

#fix capital
country_event = {
	id = prc.153
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = PRC
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = peking_capital
				controls_state = 608
				capital_scope = { NOT = { state = 608 }}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = nanking_capital
				controls_state = 613
				capital_scope = { NOT = { state = 613 }}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = peking_capital
				controls_state = 608
				capital_scope = { NOT = { state = 608 }}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nanking_capital
				controls_state = 613
				capital_scope = { NOT = { state = 613 }}
			}
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
}

#declare war on jap or not
country_event = {
	id = prc.158
	title = prc.158.t
	desc = prc.158.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_transport_soldiers
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		NOT = {	
			has_global_flag = KMT_united_front_enabled
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			has_war_with = JAP
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
			has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			has_war_together_with = JAP
			has_war_together_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			is_in_faction_with = JAP
			is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
		is_puppet = no
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		name = prc.158.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = take_core_state
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_political_power = 150
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		name = prc.158.b
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			type = civil_war
		}
		add_war_support = -0.1
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
		name = prc.158.c
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = take_core_state
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			type = civil_war
		}
		add_war_support = 0.15
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = 25
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		name = prc.158.e
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -500
	}
}

	trigger = {
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		name = prc.161.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_transfer_PRC_core_states_to_PRC_tt
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.164 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { PRC.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
				}
				PRC = { 
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		name = prc.161.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.162 }
		}
	}
}

#suppress zxl fascism
country_event = {
	id = prc.165
	title = prc.165.t
	desc = prc.165.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_leader = {
			character = ZXL_zhang_xueliang
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		NOT = { 
			has_completed_focus = PRC_destroy_mao_and_his_clique
			focus_progress = {
				focus = PRC_destroy_mao_and_his_clique
				progress > 0
			}
			has_completed_focus = PRC_trust_in_communism
			has_government = fascism
		}
		fascism > 0.33
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.165.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.25
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.025
	}
}

#deserters to chi
country_event = {
	id = prc.166
	title = prc.166.t
	desc = prc.166.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		democratic > 0.33
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			has_government = democratic
			exists = yes
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_democratic_deserters }
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = PRC_democratic_deserters
				days > 90
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 50 }
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = PRC_democratic_deserters
		set_country_flag = PRC_democratic_deserters
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
				country_event = { id = prc.165 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.166.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -1
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_manpower = -100
	}
}

#cull fascism
country_event = {
	id = prc.168
	title = prc.168.t
	desc = prc.168.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_leader = {
			character = ZXL_zhang_xueliang
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		fascism > 0.35
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = PRC_destroy_mao_and_his_clique
			has_completed_focus = PRC_trust_in_communism
			focus_progress = {
				focus = PRC_destroy_mao_and_his_clique
				progress > 0
			}
			focus_progress = {
				focus = PRC_trust_in_communism
				progress > 0
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.35
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.168.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.35
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_prc168_tt
	}
}

#mao and wang
country_event = {
	id = prc.174
	title = prc.174.t
	desc = prc.174.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_mao_wang
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		focus_progress = {
			focus = PRC_zgt_purge_focus
			progress > 0
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		name = prc.174.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_pp_award_increase2_tt
		add_to_variable = { PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter = 2 }
		set_country_flag = PRC_wang_mao_executed
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = PRC_wang_ming_executed
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 300
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 1064
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 1064
			hidden_effect = { PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.174.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_pp_award_increase_tt
		add_to_variable = { PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter = 1 }
		set_country_flag = PRC_mao_imprisoned
		set_country_flag = PRC_wang_ming_imprisoned
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = PRC_wang_ming_imprisoned
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 1064
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 1064
			hidden_effect = { PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }}
		}
		add_political_power = 150
		add_to_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_max_reactionary_hideout = 1 }
		increase_zgt_reactionary = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.174.c
		add_political_power = -150
		add_to_variable = {global.PRC_zgt_max_reactionary_hideout = 2 }
		increase_zgt_reactionary2 = yes
	}
}

#generals
country_event = {
	id = prc.175
	title = prc.175.t
	desc = prc.175.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		focus_progress = {
			focus = PRC_zgt_purge_focus
			progress > 0
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		name = prc.175.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_pp_award_increase2_tt
		add_to_variable = { PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter = 2 }
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = PRC_zgt_purge2
		set_country_flag = PRC_zgt_purge
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1065 } remove_unit_leader = 1065 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1066 } remove_unit_leader = 1066 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1068 } remove_unit_leader = 1068 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1069 } remove_unit_leader = 1069 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1070 } remove_unit_leader = 1070 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1071 } remove_unit_leader = 1071 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1072 } remove_unit_leader = 1072 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1073 } remove_unit_leader = 1073 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 2108 } remove_unit_leader = 2108 }
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC_zhu_de = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_lin_biao = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_peng_dehuai = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_xu_xiangqian = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_he_long = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_liu_bocheng = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_ye_jianying = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_nie_rongzhen = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_xiao_ke = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.175.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_pp_award_increase_tt
		add_to_variable = { PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter = 1 }
		set_country_flag = PRC_zgt_purge
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = PRC_wang_mao_executed 
					has_country_flag = PRC_mao_imprisoned 
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1072 } remove_unit_leader = 1072 }
			hidden_effect = { PRC_ye_jianying = { set_nationality = ZZZ } }
		}
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1066 } remove_unit_leader = 1066 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1070 } remove_unit_leader = 1070 }
		if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1073 } remove_unit_leader = 1073 }
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC_zhu_de = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_he_long = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			PRC_nie_rongzhen = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_max_reactionary_hideout = 1 }
		increase_zgt_reactionary = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.175.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_wooed_former_4th_general
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_available_cuz_wooed_tt
		add_command_power = 50
		add_to_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_max_reactionary_hideout = 1 }
		increase_zgt_reactionary = yes
		
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_id = 1072
					has_id = 1070
					has_id = 1066
					has_id = 1073
				}
			}
			add_timed_unit_leader_trait = {
				trait = disgruntled
				days = 30
			}
			add_timed_unit_leader_trait = {
				trait = demoted
				days = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

			base = 1
		}

		add_to_variable = { PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_max_reactionary_hideout = 1 }
		add_political_power = 100
		increase_zgt_reactionary = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter < 3 }
		}
		name = prc.176.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = prc.177
	title = prc.177.t
	desc = prc.177.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_zhang_head
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.177.a
		set_temp_variable = { PRC_pp_zgt_purge_award = 60 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { PRC_pp_zgt_purge_award = PRC_zgt_purge_brutal_meter }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { PRC_pp_zgt_purge_award = 0 }
			}
			add_political_power = 25
		}else = {
			add_political_power = PRC_pp_zgt_purge_award
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 283 }}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = PRC_take_southern_kansu
		}
	}
}

	id = prc.181
	title = prc.178.t
	desc = prc.178.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_prc_members
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.178.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = PRC_mao_zedong
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { PRC.PRC_mao_power_change = -1 }
			change_mao_power = yes
		}else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = PRC_zhang_guotao
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { PRC.PRC_zhang_power_change = -1 }
			change_zhang_power = yes
		}else = {
			set_temp_variable = { PRC.PRC_wang_power_change = -1 }
			change_wang_power = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = prc.186
	title = prc.186.t

	picture = GFX_report_event_zhang_mao
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		focus_progress = {
			focus = PRC_rise_of_wang_ming
			progress > 0
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.186.a
		set_temp_variable = { PRC_temp_wang_pp_award = 100 }
		set_temp_variable = { PRC_temp_wang_purgeV = PRC_wang_purge_mao_zhang }
		multiply_temp_variable = { PRC_temp_wang_pp_award = PRC_temp_wang_purgeV }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PRC_discredited_mao
			}
			set_country_flag = PRC_wang_purged_zhang
			set_country_flag = PRC_splinter_groups
			add_ideas = PRC_splinter_elements
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						has_resistance = yes
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = { 
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }
				}
			}else = {
				random_controlled_state = { 
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1064 } remove_unit_leader = 1064 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1084 } remove_unit_leader = 1084 }
			hidden_effect = {
				PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
				PRC_zhang_guotao = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			}
		}else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PRC_discredited_mao
			}
			set_country_flag = PRC_wang_purged_mao
			set_country_flag = PRC_splinter_groups
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						has_resistance = yes
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = { 
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_hideout }
				}
			}else = {
				random_controlled_state = { 
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_hideout }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = PRC_splinter_elements
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1064 } remove_unit_leader = 1064 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1084 } remove_unit_leader = 1084 }
			hidden_effect = {
				PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
				PRC_zhang_guotao = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			}
		}else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { PRC_wang_purge_mao_zhang > 2 }
			}
			set_country_flag = PRC_wang_purged_zhang
			set_country_flag = PRC_wang_purged_mao
			retire_character = PRC_mao_zedong
			retire_character = PRC_zhang_guotao
		}else = {
			set_country_flag = PRC_splinter_groups
			add_ideas = PRC_splinter_elements2
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						has_resistance = yes
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = { 
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }
				}
			}else = {
				random_controlled_state = { 
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = {
						has_resistance = yes
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = { 
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_hideout }
				}
			}else = {
				random_controlled_state = { 
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_hideout }
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1064 } remove_unit_leader = 1064 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1084 } remove_unit_leader = 1084 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1065 } remove_unit_leader = 1065 }
			if = { limit = { has_unit_leader = 1066 } remove_unit_leader = 1066 }
			hidden_effect = {
				PRC_zhu_de = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
				PRC_lin_biao = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
				PRC_mao_zedong = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
				PRC_zhang_guotao = { set_nationality = ZZZ }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = PRC_temp_wang_pp_award
	}
}

			progress > 0
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.187.a
		set_temp_variable = { PRC_wm_temp_autonomy = PRC_wang_sov_assistance }
		divide_temp_variable = { PRC_wm_temp_autonomy = 2 }
		round_temp_variable = PRC_wm_temp_autonomy
		set_variable = { global.PRC_comintern_autonomy = PRC_wm_temp_autonomy }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { global.PRC_comintern_autonomy > 5 }} set_variable = { global.PRC_comintern_autonomy = 5 }}
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { global.PRC_comintern_autonomy < 0 }} set_variable = { global.PRC_comintern_autonomy = 0 }}
		set_temp_variable = { PRC_wm_temp_pp_dedu = PRC_wang_sov_assistance }
		multiply_temp_variable = { PRC_wm_temp_pp_dedu = -25 }
		add_political_power = PRC_wm_temp_pp_dedu
		set_country_flag = PRC_autonomy_enabled
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PRC_dcat_autonomy_from_comintern
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_comintern_autonomy_effect_0 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_comintern_autonomy_effect_1 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_comintern_autonomy_effect_2 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_comintern_autonomy_effect_3 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_comintern_autonomy_effect_4 }

		}
	}

				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 70
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 90
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = PRC_wang_ming
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					has_equipment = { infantry_equipment < 1000 }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		name = prc.195.a 
		add_political_power = -25
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = -500 }
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = prc.196 }
			activate_mission = PRC_more_sov_aid_mission
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5

				add = 3
			}

				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
				add = 2
			}

				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -20
				}
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM

				}
				add = 3
			}

		}
	}

#detected prc cells
country_event = {
	id = prc.207
	title = prc.207.t
	desc = prc.207.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 35 }
	
	trigger = {
		has_war_with = PRC
		any_controlled_state = {
			check_variable = { THIS.PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength > 14 }
			NOT = { has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { THIS.PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength > 14 }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected }
				}
				log = "[Root.GetName]: detects PRC guerrilla cell in state [This.GetName]"
				set_state_flag = KMT_PRC_state_cell_detected
				set_variable = { var = THIS.PRC_state_estimated_cell_strength value = THIS.PRC_state_guerrilla_cell_strength }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.207.a
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PRC_dcat_pacify_enemy_guerrilla_cell
	}
}

		name = prc.211.a
		add_political_power = 150
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = 200 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		transfer_state = 753
		753 = {
			add_compliance = 35
			add_resistance = -100
		}
		set_global_flag = PRC_zgt_border_war_resolved
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PRC_yes_truce
				NOT = { has_global_flag = PRC_restart_CHI_war }
			}
			add_to_variable = { global.PRC_expansion_ire = global.PRC_expansion_ire_from_bw }
			add_to_variable = { global.PRC_expansion_ire_from_bw = 1 }
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = prc.221
	title = prc.221.t
	desc = prc.221.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.221.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = PRC_zgt_5y_civ
			days = 1825
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.221.b
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = PRC_zgt_5y_mil
			days = 1825
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.221.c
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = PRC_zgt_5y_mix
			days = 1825
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = prc.223
	title = prc.4.t
	desc = prc.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_physics_lab_02
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_1
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_2
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_3
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_4
				}
				has_completed_focus = PRC_republic_university
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_1
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_2
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_3
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_4
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_5
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_6
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
					has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
				}
				has_completed_focus = PRC_university_expansion
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 50 }
	
	option = {
		name = prc.4.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = prc_msp_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
			}
			remove_ideas = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
			add_research_slot = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_10
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_9
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_8
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_6
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_6
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_5
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_5
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_6
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_4
				add_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = PRC_lack_skilled_personnel_3

#reactionaries take hideout
country_event = {
	id = prc.224
	title = prc.224.t
	desc = prc.224.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea0
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea1
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea2
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea3
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea4
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea5
			has_idea = PRC_zgt_reactionary_remnant_idea6
		}
		num_of_controlled_states > 5
		check_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_max_reactionary_hideout > 0 }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_in_array = { ROOT.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_to_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
					set_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
				}
			}else = {
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_in_array = { ROOT.KMT_considered_inalienable_parts = THIS }
					}
					add_to_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
					set_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_current_reactionary_hideout = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.224.a
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PRC_dcat_zgt_reactionary_elements
		random_state = {
			limit = { has_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_reactionary_establish_hideout_tt
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
			}
			clr_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
		}
	}
}

#reactionaries return from overbroad
country_event = {
	id = prc.226
	title = prc.226.t
	desc = prc.226.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		any_state = {
			is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
			NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 20 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
					NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
				remove_from_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = { 
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }}
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }}
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }}
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }}
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_to_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
					set_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
				}
			}else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = { 
						any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }}
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }}
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						any_neighbor_state = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }}
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }}
					}
					add_to_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
					set_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
				}
			}else_if = {
				limit = {
					any_controlled_state = { 
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }}
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						NOT = { is_in_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }}
					}
					add_to_array = { global.PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout_array = THIS }
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
					set_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
				}
			}else = {
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					set_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout_move
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { global.PRC_zgt_current_reactionary_hideout = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.226.a
		random_state = {
			limit = { has_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_reactionary_establish_hideout_tt
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_zgt_reactionary_hideout }
			}
			clr_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = { has_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout_move }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_zgt_reactionary_move_to_hideout_tt
			clr_state_flag = PRC_zgt_reactionary_elements_hideout_move
		}
	}
}

	desc = prc.251.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		PRC = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_government = communism
		}
		SOV = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_government = communism
			NOT = { has_war_with = PRC }
		}
		NOT = {
			any_country = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
				has_war_with = PRC
			}
			any_country = {
				is_in_faction_with = PRC
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { PRC = { is_faction_leader = yes }} PRC = { dismantle_faction = yes }}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = PRC_byzantine_paperworks }
				remove_ideas = PRC_byzantine_paperworks
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = PRC
				}
				ROOT = { 
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
				}
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PRC
				autonomy_state = PRC_ssr_autonomy_status
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = prc.251.a
		remove_ideas = PRC_byzantine_paperworks
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_declare_war_on_all_prc_enemies
		set_autonomy = {
			target = PRC
			autonomy_state = PRC_ssr_autonomy_status
		}
	}
}

	desc = prc.269.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.269.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 94
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				add = 5
			}
		}
		FROM = {		
			country_event = { id = prc.270 }
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_national_defence_government_legitimacy }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_national_defence_government_legitimacy }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					FROM = { declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = puppet_wargoal_focus }}
				}
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ROOT
				autonomy_state = PRC_ssr_autonomy_status
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_declare_war_on_all_prc_enemies
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.269.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		set_country_flag = PRC_rejected_to_join_the_union
		FROM = {		
			country_event = { id = prc.271 }
		}
	}
}

	id = prc.277
	title = prc.277.t
	desc = prc.277.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_communist_leader
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_government = communism
		has_completed_focus = PRC_rise_of_wang_ming
		OR = {
			is_subject = no
			is_subject_of = SOV
		}
		SOV = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_broken_tie_with_SOV }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	option = {
		name = prc.277.a
		set_country_flag = PRC_broken_tie_with_SOV
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = SOV }
			SOV = { end_puppet = ROOT }
		}
	}
}

		NOT = { has_idea = PRC_government_corruption }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_end_capital_accumulation }
	}

country_event = {
	id = prc.289
	title = prc.289.t
	desc = prc.289.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.289.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = PRC_dismantle_ndg_betrayal
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_national_defence_government_legitimacy }
		decrease_prc_comintern_autonomy1 = yes
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			country_event = { id = prc.290 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = PRC_ordered_dismantling_of_ndg
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = prc.291 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.289.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				add = 4
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = PRC_armed_defence_of_soviet_union }
			add_war_support = -0.1
			decrease_ndglegi5 = yes
		}else = {
			decrease_ndglegi2 = yes
		}
		increase_prc_comintern_autonomy1 = yes
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = prc.292 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = PRC_refuse_to_dismantle_ndg
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = PRC_refuse_to_dismantle_ndg_trade
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = PRC_refuse_to_dismantle_ndg_prc
		}
	}
}

#2nd and 4th arrive
country_event = {
	id = prc.295
	title = prc.295.t
	desc = prc.295.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_meeting
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_country_flag = PRC_failed_24_mission
		any_state = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PRC_2nd_and_4th_rendezvoused
			division_template = {
				name = "Ch'ang-cheng Ts'an-pu"	
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 } 
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 } 
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 } 
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 } 
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 } 
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 } 
				}
			}
			
			random_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 622 }
				##### 2nd Chüntuan Group #####
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"2nd Chüntuan\" division_template = \"Ch'ang-cheng Ts'an-pu\" start_equipment_factor = 0.2" 
					owner = PRC
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"6th Chüntuan\" division_template = \"Ch'ang-cheng Ts'an-pu\" start_equipment_factor = 0.1" 
					owner = PRC
				}
	
				##### 4th Chüntuan Group #####
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"4th Chüntuan\" division_template = \"Ch'ang-cheng Ts'an-pu\" start_equipment_factor = 0.2" 
					owner = PRC
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"30th Chüntuan\" division_template = \"Ch'ang-cheng Ts'an-pu\" start_equipment_factor = 0.3" 
					owner = PRC
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"5th Chüntuan\" division_template = \"Ch'ang-cheng Ts'an-pu\" start_equipment_factor = 0.1" 
					owner = PRC
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.295.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_2nd_4th_army_arrive_tt
	}
}

#mao hideout eliminated
country_event = {
	id = prc.296
	title = prc.296.t
	desc = {
		text = prc.296.d_1
		trigger = {
			any_controlled_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = prc.296.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { any_controlled_state = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }}}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_meeting
	
	option = {
		name = prc.296.a
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = PRC_mao_hideout }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PRC = { has_idea = PRC_splinter_elements }}
			PRC = { remove_ideas = PRC_splinter_elements }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PRC = { has_idea = PRC_splinter_elements2 }}
			PRC = { 
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PRC_splinter_elements2
					add_idea = PRC_splinter_elements
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = prc.299
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { 
				has_state_flag = KMT_collaborator_state
				NOT = { has_state_flag = KMT_return_collaborator_land_weichun_spawned_state_flag }
			}
			set_state_flag = KMT_return_collaborator_land_weichun_spawned_state_flag
			create_unit = { 
				division = "name = \"Shoupien Weichün\" division_template = \"Weichün\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
				owner = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { 
				has_state_flag = KMT_collaborator_state
				has_resistance = yes
				NOT = { has_state_flag = KMT_return_collaborator_land_compliance_raised_flag }
			}
			add_compliance = 50
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
}

				defense_skill = 2
				planning_skill = 3
				logistics_skill = 3
				skill = 3
				id = 1075
			}
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Ch'en I"			#陳毅
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/Chen_Yi.dds"
				traits = { brilliant_strategist career_officer guerilla_fighter }
				attack_skill = 2
				defense_skill = 3
				planning_skill = 3
				logistics_skill = 2
				skill = 3
				id = 1067
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 2500 }
		add_manpower = 5000
		army_experience = 50
	}
}

#sino-soviet war
country_event = {
	id = prc.329
	title = prc.329.t
	desc = prc.329.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			is_subject = no
			OVERLORD = {
				is_chinese_nations_w_HYQ = yes
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			has_government = communism
			is_subject = no
		}
		OR = {
			is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			is_subject_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
			is_in_faction = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.329.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			OVERLORD = { end_puppet = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			add_stability = -0.2
			add_war_support = -0.25
		}
		add_manpower = -35000
		set_global_flag = PRC_restart_CHI_war
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = kns.49 }}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = GCDcivilwar
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				OR = {
					tag = SOV
					is_subject_of = SOV
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = SOV
					enemy = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { is_in_faction = yes }}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = prc.330 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.329.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			OVERLORD = { end_puppet = ROOT }
		}
		add_manpower = -15000
		add_stability = -0.35
		add_war_support = -0.05
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				OR = {
					tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					is_subject_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = { is_in_faction = yes }}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			country_event = { id = prc.330 }
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					enemy = SOV
					targeted_alliance = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		name = prc.329.c
		add_manpower = -50000
		random_controlled_state = { add_manpower = -50000 }
		random_controlled_state = { add_manpower = -50000 }
		random_controlled_state = { add_manpower = -50000 }
		add_war_support = -0.5
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = PRC_sino_soviet_war_deserters
			days = 600
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.329.e
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				has_war_with = SOV 
				has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag 
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

#trautmann truce
country_event = {
	id = prc.332
	title = prc.332.t
	desc = prc.332.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_rule = { can_join_factions = no }}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.332.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_ideas = PRC_anti_jap_national_salvation_uf_idea 
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_chinese_nations_w_HYQ = yes
				NOT = { 
					has_idea = KMT_trautmann_peace 
					is_subject_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
					has_war_with = ROOT
					has_country_flag = KMT_no_trautmann_peace_reactionary
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = prc.333 }
		}
		create_faction = KMT_anti_jap_national_salvation_uf
		hidden_effect = { set_rule = { can_join_factions = yes }}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = { 
					has_idea = KMT_trautmann_peace
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			diplomatic_relation = { relation = non_aggression_pact country = ROOT active = no }
			ROOT = { diplomatic_relation = { relation = non_aggression_pact country = PREV active = no }}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_idea = KMT_trautmann_peace }
			ROOT = { create_wargoal = { target = PREV type = civil_war }}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = kns.53 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.332.b
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = PRC }}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = KMT_no_trautmann_peace_reactionary
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_nations_w_HYQ = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = KMT_no_trautmann_peace_reactionary
					tag = ROOT
					has_idea = KMT_trautmann_peace 
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = prc.332 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_rule = { can_join_factions = yes }}
	}
}

#trautmann truce
country_event = {
	id = prc.333
	title = prc.333.t
	desc = prc.333.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			is_subject_of = FROM
			is_in_faction_with = FROM
			has_war_with = FROM
		}
		country_exists = FROM
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.333.a
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					ROOT = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					has_idea = KMT_trautmann_peace
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_government = fascism
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SIK_sheng_shicai
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = XIA_he_jian
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				FROM = { 
					tag = PRC
					has_government = communism
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = GXC_li_zongren
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SCC_liu_xiang
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SKC_liu_wenhui
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = YUN_long_yun
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = XIA_zhang_zhizhong
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = XIA_cheng_qian
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SDC_han_fuju
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = no }}
			FROM = { create_faction = KMT_anti_jap_national_salvation_uf }
		}
		FROM = { 
			add_to_faction = ROOT 
			country_event = { id = prc.334 }
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			country_event = { id = prc.336 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = { 
					has_idea = KMT_trautmann_peace
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			diplomatic_relation = { relation = non_aggression_pact country = ROOT active = no }
			ROOT = { diplomatic_relation = { relation = non_aggression_pact country = PREV active = no }}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = KMT_trautmann_truce_demilitarised_zone
			}
			clr_state_flag = KMT_trautmann_truce_demilitarised_zone
			if = { limit = { is_demilitarized_zone = yes } set_demilitarized_zone = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_devote_to_the_party_and_state }
			hidden_effect = {
			
				set_variable = { KMT_warlord_border_war_defender_modifier = 1 }
				set_variable = { KMT_warlord_border_war_attacker_modifier = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = KMT_proclaimed_opposition }
					clr_country_flag = KMT_proclaimed_opposition
				}
			
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_ostensible_loyalty }
					add_stability = -0.05
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_neutral_stance }
					add_stability = -0.15
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_devote_to_the_party_and_state }
					add_stability = -0.05
					add_war_support = -0.15
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_officials_screening }
					add_war_support = -0.1
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_new_model_region }
					subtract_from_variable = { global.KMT_gc_max_ip_from_loyal_warlords = 2 }
					add_stability = -0.05
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_spread_propaganda }
					add_war_support = -0.05
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_maintain_regional_presence }
					add_stability = -0.05
					add_war_support = -0.05
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = KMT_continue_regional_development }
					add_stability = -0.1
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KMT_warlord_suppress_dissidents_idea }
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_suppress_dissidents_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KMT_warlord_defensive_posture }
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_defensive_posture
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KMT_warlord_propaganda_effort }
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_propaganda_effort
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KMT_warlord_benefits_from_all_sides_idea }
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_benefits_from_all_sides_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KMT_warlord_regional_elites_idea }
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_regional_elites_idea
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KMT_warlord_home_land_defence_force_idea }
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_home_land_defence_force_idea
				}
				
				load_focus_tree = KMT_warlord_generic_focus
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = prc.333.b
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = prc.335 }
		}
	}
}

			change_mao_power = yes
		}else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = PRC_zhang_guotao ruling_only = yes }}
			set_temp_variable = { PRC.PRC_zhang_power_change = -5 }
			change_zhang_power = yes
		}else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = PRC_wang_ming ruling_only = yes }}
			set_temp_variable = { PRC.PRC_wang_power_change = -5 }
			change_wang_power = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = prc.341
	title = prc.341.t
	desc = prc.341.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = prc.341.a
		add_stability = -0.025
		add_war_support = 0.1
		army_experience = 100
		division_template = {
			name = "Kuo-chün Ts'an-pu"
			regiments = { 
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 } 
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 } 
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 } 
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 } 
			}
			support = {  }
		}
		random_controlled_state = {
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Kuo-chün Ts'an-pu\" division_template = \"Kuo-chün Ts'an-pu\" start_experience_factor = 0.65 start_equipment_factor = 0.5 force_equipment_variants = { infantry_equipment_1 = { owner = CHI } }	"
				OWNER = PRC
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no  
				count = 2
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "name = \"Kuo-chün Ts'an-pu\" division_template = \"Kuo-chün Ts'an-pu\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.33 force_equipment_variants = { infantry_equipment_0 = { owner = CHI } }	"
				OWNER = PRC
				allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = no  
				count = 3
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			every_character = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = PRC_potential_defectors }
				set_nationality = PRC
			}
		}
	}
}
